      <article class="clearfix post-22894 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-addis-pablo category-artists category-bob-marley category-bob-marley-and-the-wailers category-carlton-tetrack-hines category-chronixx category-dub-architect category-gregory-isaacs category-junior-byles category-kabaka-pyramid category-keznamdi category-lee-perry category-live-audio-and-video category-negusa-negast category-podcasts-and-mixes category-rockers category-roots-vibes category-tabou1 tag-bob-marley tag-dexta-malawi tag-dreada-dub tag-dreada-mix tag-dub-plate tag-midnight-raver tag-paul-hurlock tag-protoje tag-sly-robbie" id="post-22894">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <span class="comments-link">
         <a href="http://midnightraverblog.com/2014/10/midnight-ravers-dreada-dub-vol-7-who-seh-dub-is-dead/#respond">

         </a>
        </span>
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         Midnight Ravers DREADA DUB VOL 7:  Who Seh Dub Is Dead?
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta">
         <span class="posted-on">
          Posted on
          <a href="http://midnightraverblog.com/2014/10/midnight-ravers-dreada-dub-vol-7-who-seh-dub-is-dead/" rel="bookmark" title="4:42 am">
           <time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2014-10-13T04:42:30+00:00">
            October 13, 2014
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          by
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="http://midnightraverblog.com/author/midnightraverblog/" title="View all posts by midnightraverblog">
            midnightraverblog
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
       </header>
       <div class="clearfix entry-content">
        <p>
         The long-awaited Vol. 7 of Midnight Ravers DREADA DUB SERIES includes some of the very best dub mixes from 2014:
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="color:#ff9900;">
          <strong>
           UNRELEASED
          </strong>
         </span>
         dub mixes from Sly &amp; Robbie feat. Paul Groucho Smykle from the forthcoming
         <strong>
          <em>
           DUBRISING
          </em>
         </strong>
         LP FROM
         <span style="color:#ff9900;">
          <strong>
           TABOU1
          </strong>
         </span>
         (Jah Ravers selection for best reggae/dub LP of 2014!);
         <strong>
          <span style="color:#ff9900;">
           UNRELEASED
          </span>
         </strong>
         alternate dub mix of Tetracks smash new single
         <strong>
          <em>
           THAT DAY WILL COME
          </em>
         </strong>
         from Mr. Haze and Roots Vibes;
         <strong>
          <span style="color:#ff9900;">
           BRAND NEW UNRELEASED
          </span>
         </strong>
         killer dub mix from Tallman &amp; Binghi of Natural High Music feat. Dexta Malawi inna Midnight Raver dubplate stylee!;
         <strong>
          <span style="color:#ff9900;">
           UNRELEASED
          </span>
         </strong>
         dub track from Italys Road To Zion crew;
         <strong>
          <span style="color:#ff9900;">
           UNRELEASED
          </span>
         </strong>
         heavy dub of Keznamdis
         <strong>
          <em>
           GRADE
          </em>
         </strong>
         by Don Corleone (Ravers Best of 2014!); the highly-sought-after dub version of Protoge &amp; Chronixx on
         <strong>
          <em>
           WHO KNOWS
          </em>
         </strong>
         ; new dub mix of Kenyatta Hills
         <strong>
          <em>
           JAH IS MY FRIEND
          </em>
         </strong>
         by Dub Architect (another Best of 2014 selection!); the impossibly rare versions to Paul Hurlocks
         <strong>
          <em>
           
           <strong>
            S
           </strong>
           OMEONE CUT IT DOWN,
          </em>
         </strong>
         Big Youths
         <strong>
          <em>
           SPIDERMAN MEET HULK,
          </em>
         </strong>
         and Mike Brooks
         <strong>
          <em>
           NIGHT RAIVA;
          </em>
         </strong>
         <strong>
          <span style="color:#ff9900;">
           RARE
          </span>
         </strong>
         <strong>
          <em>
           ROOTS ROCK REGGAE
          </em>
         </strong>
         dubplate by Bob Marley &amp; the Wailers and much, much more!
        </p>
        <p>
         Big up my man
         <span style="color:#ff9900;">
          <strong>
           <em>
            DEXTA MALAWI! BINGHI, TALLMAN
           </em>
          </strong>
         </span>
         <strong>
          <em>
           and the
          </em>
         </strong>
         <span style="color:#ff9900;">
          <strong>
           <em>
            NATURAL HIGH MUSIC crew! DUB NAH DEAD!
            <br/>
           </em>
          </strong>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         CHECK FOR
         <span style="color:#ff9900;">
          <strong>
           SLY &amp; ROBBIES
          </strong>
          <em>
           <strong>
            DUBRISING
           </strong>
          </em>
         </span>
         LP NOVEMBER 2014 FROM
         <strong>
          <span style="color:#ff9900;">
           GUILLAUME BOUGARDS TABOU1 RECORDS!
          </span>
          <span style="color:#ff0000;">
           MIDNIGHT RAVERS BEST REGGAE ALBUM OF 2014!
          </span>
         </strong>
         PAUL 
         <strong>
          GROUCHO
         </strong>
          SMYKLE BACK INNA THE MIX !
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="who seh dub is dead" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-22895" height="250" src="https://marleyarkives.files.wordpress.com/2014/10/who-seh-dub-is-dead.jpg" width="545"/>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align:center;">
         <iframe frameborder="no" height="450" scrolling="no" src="https://w.soundcloud.com/player?url=https%3A%2F%2Fapi.soundcloud.com%2Ftracks%2F171785499&amp;visual=true&amp;auto_play=false&amp;hide_related=false&amp;show_comments=true&amp;show_user=true&amp;show_reposts=false" width="100%">
         </iframe>
        </p>
        <p style="text-align:center;">
         Track List:
        </p>
        <p style="text-align:center;">
         <em>
          Dexta Malawi  Woke Up Dub
         </em>
         <em>
          (Natural High Music, Jamaica)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Groucho Smykle/Sly &amp; Robbie  Double Agent (previously unreleased)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Groucho Smykle/Sly &amp; Robbie  Surrender (previously unreleased)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Keznamdi  Grade Dub (Don Corleone)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Road To Zion  Drapers
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Benny Page  Champion Sound (Samson Remix)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Protoje feat. Chronixx  Who Knows (7 Dub Mix)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Papa Levi  Inna Mi Yard (Tuff Scout)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Kabaka Pyramid feat. Suns of Dub  Weeping Dub
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Addis Pablo  His Majesty
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Addis Pablo  Rockers Version
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Subatomic Sound System  Jah Vengeance (Live)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Sizzla  A Living Dub
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Kenyatta Hill  Jah Is My Friend (Dub Architect Mix)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Protoje  Be Wise Dub
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Lee Scratch Perry  Rastafari on Wall Street
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Lee Scratch Perry  Wall Street Version
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Giant Panda Guerilla Dub Squad  Solution
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Messian Dread feat. Dennis Alcapone  Dub The Dub You Dub
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Tetrack  That Day Will Come (Unreleased Mr. Haze Alternate Mix)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Alien Dread  Circus Dub
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Gregory Isaacs  My Religion Dub
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Junior Byles  I &amp; I (Extended)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Carlton Livingston  Tale of Two Dubs
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Paul Hurlock  Cut It Down Version
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Bob Marley &amp; the Wailers  Roots Rock Reggae (Exclusive Dub Plate!)
         </em>
         <br/>
         <em>
          Mike Brooks  Night Raver Version
          <br/>
          Big Youth  Spiderman Meet Hulk Inna Rubba Dub Style
         </em>
        </p>

wpa2a.targets=[
{title:'Midnight Raver&#8217;s DREADA DUB VOL 7:  Who Seh Dub Is Dead?',url:'http://midnightraverblog.com/2014/10/midnight-ravers-dreada-dub-vol-7-who-seh-dub-is-dead/'}];
wpa2a.html_done=true;if(wpa2a.script_ready&amp;&amp;!wpa2a.done)wpa2a.init();wpa2a.script_load();

  <!-- ThumbSniper footer - start -->
  <div style="text-align:center; font-size: xx-small; padding: 7px;">
   ThumbSniper-Plugin by
   <a href="http://thumbsniper.com" title="Thomas Schulte">
    Thomas Schulte
   </a>
  </div>
  <!-- ThumbSniper footer - end -->
  <!-- ThumbSniper scripts - start -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   function thumbsniper_rel_to_abs(url){if(/^.*\#$/.test(url)) {
						return ""; //only anchor = return nothing
					}

					var qMark = String(url).search(/\?/);
					if(qMark != -1) {
						url = String(url).substring(0, qMark);
					}

					if(/^(https?|file|ftps?|mailto|javascript|data:image\/[^;]{2,9};):/i.test(url)) {
						return url; //Url is already absolute
					}

					var base_url = location.href.match(/^(.+)\/?(?:#.+)?$/)[0]+"/";
					if(url.substring(0,2) == "//") {
						return location.protocol + url;
					}else if(url.charAt(0) == "/") {
						return location.protocol + "//" + location.host + url;
					}else if(url.substring(0,2) == "./") {
						url = "." + url;
					}else if(/^\s*$/.test(url)) {
						return ""; //Empty = Return nothing
					}else {
						url = "../" + url;
					}

					url = base_url + url;
					//var i=0;
					while(/\/\.\.\//.test(url = url.replace(/[^\/]+\/+\.\.\//g,"")));

					/* Escape certain characters to prevent XSS */
					url = url.replace(/\.$/,"").replace(/\/\./g,"").replace(/"/g,"%22").replace(/'/g,"%27").replace(/&lt;/g,"%3C").replace(/&gt;/g,"%3E");

					return url;
				}

					return returnValue;
				};
